data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"def main():\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    メイン関数：コマンドライン引数を処理してLCD表示を実行\n    \u0026quot;\u0026quot;\u0026quot;\n    # コマンドライン引数の設定\n    parser = int(args.address)\n    except ValueError:\n        print(f\u0026quot;エラー: 無効なI²Cアドレス '{args.address}'\u0026quot;)\n        sys.exit(1)\n\n    # LCDディスプレイの初期化\n    lcd_display = LCDDisplay(...)\n\n <div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">概要</h2><a id="user-content-概要" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 概要" href="#概要"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">このドキュメントは、初心者向け教育教材として最適なPythonコードのコメント記載方法を定義します。
<code>lcd_display.py</code>で実践されているコメントスタイルを標準化し、他のプロジェクトにも展開可能な形式としてまとめています。</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">基本方針</h2><a id="user-content-基本方針" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 基本方針" href="#基本方針"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">目的</h3><a id="user-content-目的" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 目的" href="#目的"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>初心者が理解できる</strong>: プログラミング初心者でも処理内容を理解できる説明</li>
<li><strong>適度な情報量</strong>: コードの可読性を損なわない程度の詳細さ</li>
<li><strong>実用的な情報</strong>: 実際の使用シーンで役立つヒントや注意事項を含む</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">3. メソッド/関数のdocstring</h2><a id="user-content-3-メソッド関数のdocstring" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 3. メソッド/関数のdocstring" href="#3-メソッド関数のdocstring"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">形式（引数あり）</h3><a id="user-content-形式引数あり" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 形式（引数あり）" href="#形式引数あり"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="def method_name(self, arg1, arg2='default'):
    &quot;&quot;&quot;
    [処理内容を1行で説明]

    Args:
        arg1 (型): 引数の説明（使用例や注意事項も記載）
        arg2 (型): 引数の説明（デフォルト値の意味も説明）
    &quot;&quot;&quot;"><pre><span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">method_name</span>(<span class="pl-s1">self</span>, <span class="pl-s1">arg1</span>, <span class="pl-s1">arg2</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">'default'</span>):
    <span class="pl-s">"""</span>
<span class="pl-s">    [処理内容を1行で説明]</span>
<span class="pl-s"></span>
<span class="pl-s">    Args:</span>
<span class="pl-s">        arg1 (型): 引数の説明（使用例や注意事項も記載）</span>
<span class="pl-s">        arg2 (型): 引数の説明（デフォルト値の意味も説明）</span>
<span class="pl-s">    """</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">実例1: 初期化メソッド</h3><a id="user-content-実例1-初期化メソッド" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 実例1: 初期化メソッド" href="#実例1-初期化メソッド"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">4. インラインコメント</h2><a id="user-content-4-インラインコメント" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 4. インラインコメント" href="#4-インラインコメント"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">原則</h3><a id="user-content-原則" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 原則" href="#原則"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><strong>重要な処理</strong>: 複雑なロジックや重要な判定には必ずコメント</li>
<li><strong>初心者への配慮</strong>: ライブラリの仕様や技術的な背景を説明</li>
<li><strong>実用的なヒント</strong>: トラブルシューティング情報を含める</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">パターン1: 初期化処理</h3><a id="user-content-パターン1-初期化処理" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: パターン1: 初期化処理" href="#パターン1-初期化処理"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# RPLCDライブラリを使用してPCF8574T搭載のI²C接続LCDを初期化
# PCF8574TはPCF8574の低電圧版で、指定は'PCF8574'でOK
self.lcd = CharLCD(
    i2c_expander='PCF8574',  # PCF8574Tもこの指定で動作
    address=i2c_address,
    port=i2c_port,
    cols=16, rows=2,
    charmap=charmap,         # 文字化け時はA00に変更
    auto_linebreaks=True
)"><pre><span class="pl-c"># RPLCDライブラリを使用してPCF8574T搭載のI²C接続LCDを初期化</span>
<span class="pl-c"># PCF8574TはPCF8574の低電圧版で、指定は'PCF8574'でOK</span>
<span class="pl-s1">self</span>.<span class="pl-c1">lcd</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">CharLCD</span>(
    <span class="pl-s1">i2c_expander</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s">'PCF8574'</span>,  <span class="pl-c"># PCF8574Tもこの指定で動作</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">address</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">i2c_address</span>,
    <span class="pl-s1">port</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">i2c_port</span>,
    <span class="pl-s1">cols</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">16</span>, <span class="pl-s1">rows</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">2</span>,
    <span class="pl-s1">charmap</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-s1">charmap</span>,         <span class="pl-c"># 文字化け時はA00に変更</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">auto_linebreaks</span><span class="pl-c1">=</span><span class="pl-c1">True</span>
)</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>ポイント</strong>:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>ライブラリの仕様や互換性情報を記載</li>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">パターン2: 座標・位置指定</h3><a id="user-content-パターン2-座標位置指定" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: パターン2: 座標・位置指定" href="#パターン2-座標位置指定"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# 行の指定（1行目: (0,0), 2行目: (0,1)）
if line == 1:
    self.lcd.cursor_pos = (0, 0)
elif line == 2:
    self.lcd.cursor_pos = (0, 1)"><pre><span class="pl-c"># 行の指定（1行目: (0,0), 2行目: (0,1)）</span>
<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">line</span> <span class="pl-c1">==</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>:
    <span class="pl-s1">self</span>.<span class="pl-c1">lcd</span>.<span class="pl-c1">cursor_pos</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> (<span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">0</span>)
<span class="pl-k">elif</span> <span class="pl-s1">line</span> <span class="pl-c1">==</span> <span class="pl-c1">2</span>:
    <span class="pl-s1">self</span>.<span class="pl-c1">lcd</span>.<span class="pl-c1">cursor_pos</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> (<span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-c1">1</span>)</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>ポイント</strong>:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>ユーザー視点（1行目/2行目）とシステム視点（0/1）の対応を明示</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">パターン3: アルゴリズム説明</h3><a id="user-content-パターン3-アルゴリズム説明" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: パターン3: アルゴリズム説明" href="#パターン3-アルゴリズム説明"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# 16文字以内の場合はそのまま表示
if len(text) &lt;= 16:
    # 行をクリアしてから表示
    self.lcd.write_string(' ' * 16)  # 行をクリア
    self.lcd.cursor_pos = (0, line - 1)
    self.lcd.write_string(text)"><pre><span class="pl-c"># 16文字以内の場合はそのまま表示</span>
<span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-en">len</span>(<span class="pl-s1">text</span>) <span class="pl-c1">&lt;=</span> <span class="pl-c1">16</span>:
    <span class="pl-c"># 行をクリアしてから表示</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">self</span>.<span class="pl-c1">lcd</span>.<span class="pl-c1">write_string</span>(<span class="pl-s">' '</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-c1">16</span>)  <span class="pl-c"># 行をクリア</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">self</span>.<span class="pl-c1">lcd</span>.<span class="pl-c1">cursor_pos</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> (<span class="pl-c1">0</span>, <span class="pl-s1">line</span> <span class="pl-c1">-</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>)
    <span class="pl-s1">self</span>.<span class="pl-c1">lcd</span>.<span class="pl-c1">write_string</span>(<span class="pl-s1">text</span>)</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>ポイント</strong>:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>条件分岐の意図を説明</li>
<li>各ステップの目的を明示</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">パターン4: バグ対策・特殊処理</h3><a id="user-content-パターン4-バグ対策特殊処理" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: パターン4: バグ対策・特殊処理" href="#パターン4-バグ対策特殊処理"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

self.lcd.backlight_enabled = True"><pre><span class="pl-c"># バックライトを明示的に有効化（一部基板で必要）</span>
<span class="pl-s1">self</span>.<span class="pl-c1">lcd</span>.<span class="pl-c1">backlight_enabled</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">True</span></pre></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">パターン5: ループ処理の説明</h3><a id="user-content-パターン5-ループ処理の説明" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: パターン5: ループ処理の説明" href="#パターン5-ループ処理の説明"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# 文字列の末尾にスペースを追加してループしやすくする
scroll_text = text + &quot;    &quot;

# スクロール表示（文字列を一周表示）
for i in range(len(scroll_text)):
    # 表示する16文字の部分を取得
    display_part = scroll_text[i:i+16]

    # 16文字に満たない場合は先頭から補完
    if len(display_part) &lt; 16:
        display_part += scroll_text[:16-len(display_part)]"><pre><span class="pl-c"># 文字列の末尾にスペースを追加してループしやすくする</span>
<span class="pl-s1">scroll_text</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">text</span> <span class="pl-c1">+</span> <span class="pl-s">"    "</span>

<span class="pl-c"># スクロール表示（文字列を一周表示）</span>
<span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-en">range</span>(<span class="pl-en">len</span>(<span class="pl-s1">scroll_text</span>)):
    <span class="pl-c"># 表示する16文字の部分を取得</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">display_part</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">scroll_text</span>[<span class="pl-s1">i</span>:<span class="pl-s1">i</span><span class="pl-c1">+</span><span class="pl-c1">16</span>]

    <span class="pl-c"># 16文字に満たない場合は先頭から補完</span>
    <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-en">len</span>(<span class="pl-s1">display_part</span>) <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">16</span>:
        <span class="pl-s1">display_part</span> <span class="pl-c1">+=</span> <span class="pl-s1">scroll_text</span>[:<span class="pl-c1">16</span><span class="pl-c1">-</span><span class="pl-en">len</span>(<span class="pl-s1">display_part</span>)]</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>ポイント</strong>:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>データ加工の意図を説明</li>
<li>ループ処理全体の目的を記載</li>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">実例</h3><a id="user-content-実例-3" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 実例" href="#実例-3"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="def main():
    &quot;&quot;&quot;
    メイン関数：コマンドライン引数を処理してLCD表示を実行
    &quot;&quot;&quot;
    # コマンドライン引数の設定
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(...)

    # I²Cアドレスの変換（文字列から整数へ）
    try:
        if args.address.startswith('0x'):
            i2c_addr = int(args.address, 16)
        else:
            i2c_addr = int(args.address)
    except ValueError:
        print(f&quot;エラー: 無効なI²Cアドレス '{args.address}'&quot;)
        sys.exit(1)

    # LCDディスプレイの初期化
    lcd_display = LCDDisplay(...)

    try:
        # 実行モードに応じた処理
        if args.clear:
            # 画面クリアモード
            lcd_display.clear_display()

        elif args.test:
            # テストモード
            print(&quot;テスト表示を開始します...&quot;)
            ...

    except KeyboardInterrupt:
        print(&quot;\n\n割り込み信号を受信しました。終了処理を実行中...&quot;)

    finally:
        # 必ずリソースをクリーンアップ
        lcd_display.close()"><pre><span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">main</span>():
    <span class="pl-s">"""</span>
<span class="pl-s">    メイン関数：コマンドライン引数を処理してLCD表示を実行</span>
<span class="pl-s">    """</span>
    <span class="pl-c"># コマンドライン引数の設定</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">parser</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">argparse</span>.<span class="pl-c1">ArgumentParser</span>(...)

    <span class="pl-c"># I²Cアドレスの変換（文字列から整数へ）</span>
    <span class="pl-k">try</span>:
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">args</span>.<span class="pl-c1">address</span>.<span class="pl-c1">startswith</span>(<span class="pl-s">'0x'</span>):
            <span class="pl-s1">i2c_addr</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">int</span>(<span class="pl-s1">args</span>.<span class="pl-c1">address</span>, <span class="pl-c1">16</span>)
        <span class="pl-k">else</span>:
            <span class="pl-s1">i2c_addr</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">int</span>(<span class="pl-s1">args</span>.<span class="pl-c1">address</span>)
    <span class="pl-k">except</span> <span class="pl-v">ValueError</span>:
        <span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">f"エラー: 無効なI²Cアドレス '<span class="pl-s1"><span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-s1">args</span>.<span class="pl-c1">address</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span></span>'"</span>)
        <span class="pl-s1">sys</span>.<span class="pl-c1">exit</span>(<span class="pl-c1">1</span>)

    <span class="pl-c"># LCDディスプレイの初期化</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">lcd_display</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">LCDDisplay</span>(...)

    <span class="pl-k">try</span>:
        <span class="pl-c"># 実行モードに応じた処理</span>
        <span class="pl-k">if</span> <span class="pl-s1">args</span>.<span class="pl-c1">clear</span>:
            <span class="pl-c"># 画面クリアモード</span>
            <span class="pl-s1">lcd_display</span>.<span class="pl-c1">clear_display</span>()

        <span class="pl-k">elif</span> <span class="pl-s1">args</span>.<span class="pl-c1">test</span>:
            <span class="pl-c"># テストモード</span>
            <span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">"テスト表示を開始します..."</span>)
            ...

    <span class="pl-k">except</span> <span class="pl-v">KeyboardInterrupt</span>:
        <span class="pl-en">print</span>(<span class="pl-s">"<span class="pl-cce">\n</span><span class="pl-cce">\n</span>割り込み信号を受信しました。終了処理を実行中..."</span>)

    <span class="pl-k">finally</span>:
        <span class="pl-c"># 必ずリソースをクリーンアップ</span>
        <span class="pl-s1">lcd_display</span>.<span class="pl-c1">close</span>()</pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">重要ポイント</h3><a id="user-content-重要ポイント-4" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 重要ポイント" href="#重要ポイント-4"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">エラーハンドリング</h3><a id="user-content-エラーハンドリング" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: エラーハンドリング" href="#エラーハンドリング"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul class="contains-task-list">
<li class="task-list-item"><input type="checkbox" id="" disabled="" class="task-list-item-checkbox" aria-label="Incomplete task"> エラーメッセージに処理名が含まれているか</li>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">9. プロジェクト別カスタマイズ</h2><a id="user-content-9-プロジェクト別カスタマイズ" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: 9. プロジェクト別カスタマイズ" href="#9-プロジェクト別カスタマイズ"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
